    1342              : /*--
    1343              :    The following is an implementation of
    1344              :    an elegant 3-way quicksort for strings,
    1345              :    described in a paper "Fast Algorithms for
    1346              :    Sorting and Searching Strings", by Robert

    1349              : 
    1350              : #define mswap(zz1, zz2) \
    1351              :    { Int32 zztmp = zz1; zz1 = zz2; zz2 = zztmp; }
    1352              : 
    1353              : #define mvswap(zzp1, zzp2, zzn)       \
    1354              : {                                     \
    1355              :    Int32 yyp1 = (zzp1);               \
    1356              :    Int32 yyp2 = (zzp2);               \
    1357              :    Int32 yyn  = (zzn);                \
    1358              :    while (yyn > 0) {                  \
    1359              :       mswap(ptr[yyp1], ptr[yyp2]);    \
    1360              :       yyp1++; yyp2++; yyn--;          \
    1361              :    }                                  \
    1362              : }

    1364              : static

    1366            0 : UChar mmed3 ( UChar a, UChar b, UChar c )
    1367              : {
    1368              :    UChar t;
    1369            0 :    if (a > b) { t = a; a = b; b = t; };

    1371            0 :       b = c;

    1373              :    }

    1885              : /*---------------------------------------------------*/
    1886              : #define WEIGHTOF(zz0)  ((zz0) & 0xffffff00)
    1887              : #define DEPTHOF(zz1)   ((zz1) & 0x000000ff)
    1888              : #define MYMAX(zz2,zz3) ((zz2) > (zz3) ? (zz2) : (zz3))
    1889              : 
    1890              : #define ADDWEIGHTS(zw1,zw2)                           \
    1891              :    (WEIGHTOF(zw1)+WEIGHTOF(zw2)) |                    \
    1892              :    (1 + MYMAX(DEPTHOF(zw1),DEPTHOF(zw2)))
    1893              : 
    1894              : #define UPHEAP(z)                                     \
    1895              : {                                                     \
    1896              :    Int32 zz, tmp;                                     \
    1897              :    zz = z; tmp = heap[zz];                            \
    1898              :    while (weight[tmp] < weight[heap[zz >> 1]]) {      \
    1899              :       heap[zz] = heap[zz >> 1];                       \
    1900              :       zz >>= 1;                                       \
    1901              :    }                                                  \
    1902              :    heap[zz] = tmp;                                    \
    1903              : }
    1904              : 
    1905              : #define DOWNHEAP(z)                                   \
    1906              : {                                                     \
    1907              :    Int32 zz, yy, tmp;                                 \
    1908              :    zz = z; tmp = heap[zz];                            \
    1909              :    while (True) {                                     \
    1910              :       yy = zz << 1;                                   \
    1911              :       if (yy > nHeap) break;                          \
    1912              :       if (yy < nHeap &&                               \
    1913              :           weight[heap[yy+1]] < weight[heap[yy]])      \
    1914              :          yy++;                                        \
    1915              :       if (weight[tmp] < weight[heap[yy]]) break;      \
    1916              :       heap[zz] = heap[yy];                            \
    1917              :       zz = yy;                                        \
    1918              :    }                                                  \
    1919              :    heap[zz] = tmp;                                    \
    1920              : }

    4981              :       performing several non-trivial transformations on it.  
    4982              :       Unless you are 100% familiar with *all* the algorithms 
    4983              :       contained herein, and with the consequences of modifying them, 
    4984              :       you should NOT meddle with the compression or decompression 
    4985              :       machinery.  Incorrect changes can and very likely *will* 
    4986              :       lead to disasterous loss of data.
    4987              : 
    4988              :    DISCLAIMER:
    4989              :       I TAKE NO RESPONSIBILITY FOR ANY LOSS OF DATA ARISING FROM THE
    4990              :       USE OF THIS PROGRAM, HOWSOEVER CAUSED.
    4991              : 
    4992              :       Every compression of a file implies an assumption that the
    4993              :       compressed file can be decompressed to reproduce the original.
    4994              :       Great efforts in design, coding and testing have been made to
    4995              :       ensure that this program works correctly.  However, the
    4996              :       complexity of the algorithms, and, in particular, the presence
    4997              :       of various special cases in the code which occur with very low
    4998              :       but non-zero probability make it impossible to rule out the
    4999              :       possibility of bugs remaining in the program.  DO NOT COMPRESS
    5000              :       ANY DATA WITH THIS PROGRAM AND/OR LIBRARY UNLESS YOU ARE PREPARED 
    5001              :       TO ACCEPT THE POSSIBILITY, HOWEVER SMALL, THAT THE DATA WILL 
    5002              :       NOT BE RECOVERABLE.
    5003              : 
    5004              :       That is not to say this program is inherently unreliable.
    5005              :       Indeed, I very much hope the opposite is true.  bzip2/libbzip2
    5006              :       has been carefully constructed and extensively tested.
    5007              : 
    5008              :    PATENTS:
    5009              :       To the best of my knowledge, bzip2/libbzip2 does not use any 
    5010              :       patented algorithms.  However, I do not have the resources 
    5011              :       available to carry out a full patent search.  Therefore I cannot 
    5012              :       give any guarantee of the above statement.

    5982              : /*---------------------------------------------*/
    5983              : /* Copy modification date, access date, permissions and owner from the
    5984              :    source to destination file.  We have to copy this meta-info off
    5985              :    into fileMetaInfo before starting to compress / decompress it,
    5986              :    because doing it afterwards means we get the wrong access time.
    5987              : 
    5988              :    To complicate matters, in compress() and decompress() below, the
    5989              :    sequence of tests preceding the call to saveInputFileMetaInfo()
    5990              :    involves calling fileExists(), which in turn establishes its result
    5991              :    by attempting to fopen() the file, and if successful, immediately
    5992              :    fclose()ing it again.  So we have to assume that the fopen() call
    5993              :    does not cause the access time field to be updated.
    5994              : 
    5995              :    Reading of the man page for stat() (man 2 stat) on RedHat 7.2 seems
    5996              :    to imply that merely doing open() will not affect the access time.
    5997              :    Therefore we merely need to hope that the C library only does
    5998              :    open() as a result of fopen(), and not any kind of read()-ahead
    5999              :    cleverness.
    6000              : 
    6001              :    It sounds pretty fragile to me.  Whether this carries across
    6002              :    robustly to arbitrary Unix-like platforms (or even works robustly
    6003              :    on this one, RedHat 7.2) is unknown to me.  Nevertheless ...  
    6004              : */
